[70] "Certainly."
[71] "Regarding the previously mentioned poisoning delusion, can you explain it in more detail, Rie?"
[72] Meiji asked Rie.
[73] After all, it was Rie's area of expertise - a psychiatrist.
[74] "Poisoning delusion, also known as delusion of poisoning in English, is a type of delusion disorder."
[75] "Delusion disorder?"
[76] "Previously, this disease was called schizophrenia. The clinical symptoms include easy delusions, frequent hallucinations, cognitive impairment, emotional coldness and depression, speech impairment, lack of motivation in life and work, and so on. Of course, a patient will not exhibit all of these symptoms, and the specific clinical symptoms vary from person to person."
[77] "What are some specific examples of delusions?"
[78] "The ones who always think someone is trying to harm them are called persecutory delusions. The ones who are always suspicious that their partner will cheat are called jealous delusions. The ones who always think they have an incurable illness and are soon to die are called hypochondriac delusions. The ones who think they have committed a crime are called criminal delusions. The ones who think their thoughts are being read by others are called thought broadcasting delusions. The ones who think the world is about to end when garbage falls on the road are called paranoid delusions. The ones who think they are gods or descendants of famous people are called bloodline delusions. In addition to this, delusion content is also divided into various categories."
[79] "For example, in the case of poison delusion, patients always associate poisoning with trivial matters. A strange taste in food is evidence of poisoning. The incorrect placement of utensils is also evidence of poisoning. In short, any event can become evidence of poisoning. Although it may seem strange to outsiders, the patient's subjective world does not mix virtual and reality. If the symptoms worsen, hallucinations may occur, but those smells and tastes do not actually exist. This is a very unpleasant experience for both the patient and those around them."
[80] Rei smiled as she spoke.
[81] "The appearance and content of her speech were too out of balance."
[82] "What is the cause of the illness?"
[83] "To be honest, the specific cause of the disease is not yet clear. However, research has found that patients with the disease have an excess of dopamine, a substance that spreads neurostimulation between nerve cells, in their brains. High levels of dopamine are mainly due to personality factors, such as excessive stress or extreme personality traits, which are believed to be complexly related to the disease. However, the exact mechanism is still unclear. But ultimately, excessive dopamine is very susceptible to disease, external pressure activates dopamine, and dopamine secretion further strengthens external pressure, leading to symptom exacerbation. This leads to a vicious cycle."
[84] "Is there a treatment for it?"
[85] "If treated properly, it can be cured. The proportion of patients with bipolar disorder is only about 1% of the population, and it is not a special disease. The number of patients with duodenal ulcers and gastric ulcers is roughly the same as this disease. It is a very common disease, not an intractable mystery or a terrifying disease."
[86] "If the doctor diagnoses, will dysregulation syndrome be diagnosed?"
[87] "Do you mean she should come to our hospital for a check-up?"
[88] "If so, she will probably be angry if you tell her to go to the hospital now. In this situation, a person with high self-esteem is needed at the right time…"
[89] Mingshi immediately thought of a way.

[91] "Okay, but will the tea party be English-style?"

He kept this habit after returning to Japan, and Juubun-san very much liked her grandfather. They spent a lot of time together when she was young, so she inherited this habit. Now she often invites people over for afternoon tea."

Since it was tilted forward and backward, from the front of the house, you wouldn't notice the tilt of the house. If you wanted to hide the fact that the house was tilted, that would explain Zhu Měi's strange behavior, both in the past and in the present. If you use a teacup to pour red tea, you would expose the fact that the house is tilted at the same time. Not using a plastic bottle but an aluminum can bottle is also because it would expose the fact that the house is tilted. Zhu Měi has always loved this house that has accompanied her from birth to adulthood and cannot tolerate any flaws in it. However, this year, the house tilted due to uneven subsidence in the foundation, and it is possible that Zhu Měi wanted to hide the fact that the house was tilted. But since she wanted to hide the fact that the house was tilted, it was very dangerous to hold a tea party at this time. Pouring red tea into the teacup would likely expose the fact that the house is tilted. But Zhu Měi didn't want to cancel this tea party, influenced by her grandfather who loved her, she had the habit of drinking tea since childhood. In order to hide the fact that the house was tilted and still hold the tea party, Zhu Měi thought of a compromise solution, which was to use an aluminum can of red tea at the tea party. Zhu Měi drank tea while secretly observing the guests at the tea party, which was because she was afraid that someone would notice the fact that the house was tilted, and she was filled with anxiety. Therefore, Zhu Měi was not afraid of being poisoned, and someone was lying."
[590] "Is it Jià Shòu?"
[591] "Yes. She said she was afraid of being poisoned by Mrs. Maruyama's strange behavior. But actually, Mrs. Maruyama was trying to hide the tilt of the house. Living under the same roof every day, cooking, washing clothes, bathing, and washing, there are countless opportunities to come into contact with water, and she would not have failed to notice the tilt. Therefore, she must have known the reason for Mrs. Maruyama's strange behavior. Kozue said that Mrs. Maruyama suspected her of poisoning, which is clearly her fabricated lie. Mrs. Maruyama hated Kozue's cooking, and all the meals were ordered out, which is also Kozue's lie. Mrs. Maruyama only drinks canned tea when she entertains guests.
[592] Moreover, Kozue's lie is not easily exposed. [593] That's right.

[606] "Mutoh was completely confused again."
[607] "Kobayashi set up the mechanism as follows: First, she laid another carpet of the same pattern on top of the carpet in the studio while the mistress was away. This could be moved from another room. Before the tea party began, Fujiko asked about the missing carpet in the guest room. Kobayashi replied that it had been stained and sent for cleaning, but in fact, it was placed on top of the carpet in the studio. Since the mistress had no suspicion of being poisoned, she accepted the capsule from Kobayashi without any doubt. Then, Kobayashi went to the studio, opened the can, and mixed cyanide potassium into the tea, leaving the tea stain on the carpet by the right wall of the room. Of course, the first carpet was above the second one, which remained very clean underneath. After that, she rolled up the first carpet from right to left. Since the studio had no furniture, this was possible. However, due to the inclination of the floor, the carpet would unfold and return to its original position. Therefore, ice cubes were placed as a blocker to prevent it from returning to its original position. There was an ice bucket used to cool the canned tea at the tea party? It was filled with ice cubes? At that time, it could be used. Then, an empty can of tea was placed in the center hole of the rolled carpet. The carpet was kept at the left end of the studio. Because the carpet's pile was very short, it could be easily rolled up very tightly. Because the left wall of the room was a large glass window covered by curtains, the rolled carpet was hidden behind the curtains, so it would not be noticed if not closely observed.
[608] At 5:00 p.m., Mutoh brought the mistress back to her room. Neither Mutoh nor the mistress noticed that there was a rolled carpet hidden behind the curtains on the left side of the studio. Mutoh saw the clean carpet that was originally in the studio. At 5:30 p.m., the capsule in the mistress's stomach dissolved, and cyanide potassium immediately took effect and killed her. On the other hand, the ice cubes used as the blocker in the studio melted. Due to the inclination of the floor, the rolled carpet automatically unfolded and returned to its original position. Thus, the empty can and the tea stain appeared on the carpet by the right wall of the room.
[609] Fujimoto clearly explained the mechanism that disappeared when its function was completed.

Carpets and ice are common household items, and they are indeed suitable for a maid to establish an alibi. [611] Fengyuan clearly explained the process of the device that disappeared at the same time.

[623] Translation Notes:
[624] 1. This text is likely a translation of a Japanese mystery story, which is highly praised by fans of the original work. Although it uses a common plot device, the novelty lies in its unique approach to the mystery and the clever way the clues are connected. As a short story, this is a significant achievement. Despite the somewhat clichéd ending, it can be considered a quality example of new-style Japanese mystery writing.
[625] 2. After reading the story again, one might find that the reasoning presented in it is not entirely realistic. Golden Wool criticized the logic, suggesting that the house's tilt of five degrees would create a height difference of 8.7 cm, which would be visible even without liquid. Therefore, the central argument of the story, that the choice of canned tea was made to conceal the house's tilt, is not valid.
[626] 3. Then he mentioned that if we imagine the tilt of the house to be very gentle, then the subsequent trick of making the carpet disappear through the tilt of the house will not be valid again. Because the material of the carpet is heavy, when it is rolled up, it needs to overcome a large friction force, so it is very difficult (even when a person unfolds it, a lot of force is required) for the rolled-up carpet to automatically unfold to its original state. Therefore, this trick is very difficult to complete. Of course, these are just Wool Garden's opinions, after all, it is new detective fiction, too serious and you will lose.

Of course, there are still clues that show Mr. Nakajima=Nakajima=Mr. Matsushita. The day after the incident, Mr. Matsushita saw the search team and told Chief Inspector Ogiwara, 'I've been waiting for you.' But, isn't that strange? When you think about it carefully…"
[1026] "What's strange about it?"
[1027] "The search team was all dressed in civilian clothes and didn't even have their badges. Moreover, Chief Inspector Daikichi was short and skinny, while his subordinate, Forensic Department Chief Shinsuke, was tall and had sharp eyes, and looked more like a detective. And yet, Matsutani, who should have met them for the first time, immediately recognized Daikichi as his superior. Why? Because he had already met him in another identity—Komoda Tetsuji and the Chief Inspector."
[1028] "Ah."
[1029] "The day after the incident, Matsutani yawned while on duty at the art museum. It wasn't because he said "my girlfriend didn't let me sleep last night," but because he stayed up until dawn answering police questions as Komoda. Matsutani wears a watch on his left wrist, which means he is right-handed. However, the day after the incident, in the special collection room, he used his left hand to take down the bronze mirror. As a right-hander, why did he use his left hand? That's because Matsutani became Komoda and injured his right shoulder during that time."
[1030] "But Komoda and Matsutani look completely different. Komoda has a big face, no hair on his head, and a small mustache on his upper lip. Matsutani has long hair that falls to his shoulders."
[1031] "It's easy to make your cheeks look bigger by putting cotton in your mouth. Moreover, Sōta is naturally bald, so he keeps his hair as it is when he acts as the director of the gallery and wears a wig when he acts as Sōta. Of course, the mustache is also glued on. Sōta is around forty years old, and by putting wrinkles and spots on his face, he can disguise himself as someone in his fifties. Nakatō losing his voice due to an accident is definitely fake. One can disguise their appearance through makeup, but it's not so easy to disguise one's voice. Unless a professional voice actor is involved, it's difficult to separate voices.
[1032] Ming Shì and Rī Hui still looked confused.
[1033] "It's hard to believe, but it's the truth," Shikashi interjected. "We kept a close watch on Sōta-daibanshi for four days as per Fukuzawa-san's instructions. After Sōta returned to his apartment in Nakano an hour later, Nakatō came out of that apartment. I called out to him, "Sōta-san," and he looked like he was about to deny it, but then he nodded sadly.
[1034] "Nakatō and Sōta are the same person. . . . But which one is the original?" Rī Hui asked, blinking her eyes.
[1035] "Nakatō handed over the management of the art gallery to the staff and only appeared there two to three times a month. This suggests that Sōta-daibanshi is his original identity. Instead of playing two roles, it would be more accurate to say that Nakatō Keiji is a persona he created himself. Sōta works at the gallery as his true self, appearing as Nakatō Keiji only two or three times a month, of course, he must take time off during those periods."
[1036] "So, when Nakamura Tetsuhiro touched the F system's sensor..."
[1037] "The system recognized him as Sōtai Takao and opened the door."
[1038] "So, Nakamura's fingerprints must have belonged to someone else."
[1039] "Yes. Once we realized this, it was easy to solve the puzzle of the three suspects. The three suspects - Sōtai Takao, Nakamura Tetsuhiro, and Kamiya Nobuo - Sōtai entered after the time of the victim's death, so he could not have committed the crime. Kamiya has acute terror, so he could not have committed the crime. The remaining one has a twisted right shoulder and is still unable to commit the crime. However, now we know that Nakamura Tetsuhiro is Sōtai Takao. The one with the twisted right shoulder is Sōtai, and the fingerprints of Nakamura Tetsuhiro belong to someone else. Therefore, the person who holds Nakamura Tetsuhiro's fingerprints is the killer."
[1040] "So, who is the person who holds Nakamura Tetsuhiro's fingerprints?"
[1041] "Who is it that has met both Sugao Oshiro and Jiro Nakagawa?"
[1042] "Who?"
[1043] "Higashiyama Nobuko. She said, 'Sugao-san appeared in the director's office around 9:40 pm last night and greeted the director and me before leaving.' This statement is obviously a lie. She had to keep the secret of Jiro Nakagawa being Sugao Oshiro. Therefore, she is the one who provided Jiro Nakagawa's fingerprint, and the person who provided the fingerprint is the culprit."
[1044] Shizuko couldn't help but admire Fujishima's quick thinking, pointing out the killer from a small piece of information that the investigation team had overlooked.
[1045] "What was the situation when Shiozaki Jun'ichi gave the 'Sleeping Sphinx' to his colleagues and asked if they noticed anything strange about it?"
[1046] "Shiroki handed the statue to his colleagues to collect their fingerprints."
[1047] "Collect fingerprints?"
[1048] "Shiroki may have had a trigger to suspect that Nakatani Takao and Sugawara Taeko were the same person. The simplest way to confirm that they are the same person is to check if their fingerprints match. The 'Sleeping Sphinx' is a bronze artifact with a smooth surface, making it easy to leave fingerprints. Shiroki gave the bronze statue to someone else and then collected their fingerprint. The purpose was achieved by collecting the fingerprints of Nakatani and Sugawara, but it would have been suspicious to only give the statue to these two – no, actually to one person. To cover his real purpose, he had to give the statue to other employees as well. Shiroki thus confirmed Nakatani=Takao. Shiroki's next question was: who provided the fingerprint for Nakatani Takao? At that moment, the image of Kuroda Nobuko appeared in his mind. Kuroda Nobuko had probably said something like "Sugawara Taeko came to greet the director and me when we were working together" before. Shinji realized that she was lying and quickly understood that she had to keep the secret of Nakatani=Takao and provide the fingerprint for Nakatani Takao. From Kuroda Nobuko's perspective, she said that to emphasize that Nakatani and Sugawara were two different people, but in the end, it ended up costing her life. On the evening of January 26th, after 8:00 p.m., Shinji called Kuroda Nobuko to the front of the special collection room and forced her to press her finger on the sensor of the F system. The door opened. Having already confirmed that Kuroda Nobuko was the one who provided the fingerprint for Nakatani Takao, Shinji threatened her in the special collection room. In a moment of impulse, Kuroda Nobuko stabbed Shinji Purei with a 15th-century Turkish knife from the collection. After she regained her senses, she dropped the knife and ran out of the special collection room. The record of Nakatani Takao's entry and exit between 8:34 and 8:56 p.m. on the F system actually shows that Kuroda Nobuko entered and exited the special collection room.
[1049] Shinji added, "According to Kuroda Nobuko's confession, Shinji forced her to date him. Shinji estimated that Kuroda Nobuko would sacrifice herself to protect Sugawara. Among Kuroda Nobuko and Sugawara Taeko, Kuroda Nobuko was the one who was easier to threaten."
[1050] "So that's it. After Kuroda Nobuko left the special collection room, she confessed her crime to Sugawara Taeko and Sugawara Taeko decided to protect her."
[1051] "Matsuda first entered the special collection room to confirm the situation. This is the record of Matsuda entering and exiting the special collection room between 9:11 pm and 9:18 pm. During this time, Matsuda carefully checked for any traces that could expose Ms. Takano's crime. He may have also wiped off the fingerprints on the knife. Since Ms. Takano's entry and exit to the special collection room between 8:34 pm and 8:56 pm was recorded as Nakauchi's behavior by the F system, Nakauchi had to appear at the art gallery later. If Nakauchi did not appear, leaving only the record of his entry and exit, it would arouse suspicion. Therefore, Matsuda disguised himself as Nakauchi in the director's room. - Oh, I heard that the disguise props were found in the director's room?"
[1052] "Takashi nodded and said, "The director's clothes, cotton stuffed in the mouth to make the face look bigger, a small mustache, and some makeup necessary for disguise were all found. It seems that they were kept there to be able to disguise as Nakauchi at any time."
[1053] "Matsuda disguised as Nakauchi appeared in front of Kumagai Shin'ichi and told him that he came to the art gallery after 7 pm and worked with Ms. Takano in the director's room. Then he added that he entered and exited the special collection room once between 8:34 pm and 8:56 pm, and his testimony was complete. Kumagai highly respected the director, so he would undoubtedly believe what Nakauchi said. On the other hand, in order to create the illusion that Matsuda had gone home, Ms. Takano lied and claimed that Matsuda Taichi appeared in the director's room at 9:40 pm and left. Ms. Takano's phone call to Matsuda Taichi in front of the search team was a perfect performance. There was no one on the other end of the phone, and she was acting alone. The police wanted to question Matsuda, but Matsuda was now Nakauchi, so he couldn't appear immediately. Therefore, Ms. Takano pretended to make a phone call, making the police believe that Matsuda was with his lover and could only come later, but that lover didn't even exist! When dawn came, Nakauchi should have been released from police investigation and allowed to go home, so he could reappear as Matsuda Taichi."
[1054] "Makoto felt deeply and said, "Matsuda went to such lengths to protect Ms. Takano, even risking being considered an accomplice. Why did he do that?... Could it be that Matsuda and Ms. Takano were lovers?"
[1055] "That's right." Takashi answered.
[1056] "Ata and Chiaki were lovers in high school. After breaking up over a small matter, they attended different universities and got married. It was years later, five years ago, that they met again at a high school reunion. At that time, Ata's wife had died in an accident, and Chiaki had divorced her husband for infidelity. The two of them resumed their relationship, and it seemed that they deeply loved each other. Now, they are willing to protect each other and even testify falsely in order to reduce the other's crime."
[1057] "Why did Tadao Saito initially decide to play both the roles of Saito and Nakamura?"
[1058] "Ten years ago, when Sato traveled to the United States, he met Nakagawa by chance and the two hit it off. Six years ago, Nakagawa's wife passed away from cancer, and the two decided to use her inheritance to build an art museum in Japan to fulfill their dream. For this, Nakagawa returned to Japan five years ago. However, what no one expected was that Nakagawa suddenly died soon after. It seemed that his heart was already weak, which led to sudden heart failure. The worst part was that Nakagawa did not leave a will, so his inheritance would be confiscated by the state. Sato then began his "Sato-Nakagawa" dual-life plan. Although this plan was bold, Nakagawa had lived in the United States for over 20 years and had only Sato as a friend in Japan, so things became easier. Sato secretly transported Nakagawa's body to the mountains at night and buried it. The art museum was completed, and in the F system, it was necessary to have Nakagawa Tetsuji's fingerprint, so Fujiko provided her own fingerprint. Nakagawa Tetsuji's existence was made possible by Sato's disguised body and Fujiko's provided fingerprint. The two collaborated to create a non-existent 'existence.'"
[1059] "Who exactly called the police department at 12:00 a.m. on the 27th?"
[1060] "It is Matsushita. The purpose of the call is that he wants the police to be able to accurately infer the time of death of the victim. If the body is found too late, the inferred time of death will be more vague. This way, if Matsushita's movements in and out of the scene fall within the inferred time of death, he loses the condition of being excluded from the list of suspects. To prevent this from happening, he must allow the police to be able to infer the time of death as accurately as possible."
[1061] "But if that's the case, why did he call four to three hours after the incident? Wouldn't it be better to call earlier?"
[1062] "Rie also nodded and said, "Mr. Tōyama said that if the killer didn't do this, they would be exposed soon. What's going on?"
[1063] "The apartment owner sniffed the aroma of tea and put down the cup, smiling, "If calling earlier is better, why did the criminal wait until four to three hours after the incident to call? That's because the criminal wanted the police to start searching on the 27th."
[1064] "Want the police to start searching on the 27th?"
[1065] "Yes. Nakatani Tetsu touched the sensor of the F system and was recorded as Sōtai's action. When the police arrived at the scene, they would certainly make Nakatani Tetsu, the gallery director, act as a guide. Of course, touching the sensor of the F system was inevitable. What if it was still the 26th when the incident happened? The police would investigate the entry and exit records of the special collection room on the 26th and find that Nakatani Tetsu touched the sensor when he led them into the scene, and Nakatani=Tetsai would be exposed immediately. To avoid this, Nakatani Tetsu must be the 27th when he touches the sensor to lead the police into the crime scene. In this way, the police who only care about the entry and exit records on the 26th would not discover this secret. Therefore, the criminal must wait until four to three hours after the incident, change the date, and then make the call."
[1066] C's Will
[1067] Original work: YAMAMOTO Seiji / Translation: Fang Qinjing
[1068] This short story is included in YAMAMOTO Seiji's library edition "Alphabet Puzzles" (Tokyo Sorensha) published in June 2013, and the differences from the 2004 single volume edition are that YAMAMOTO Seiji wrote this short story titled "C's Will" especially for the library edition. Additionally, according to the arrangement of the library edition, the order of the short stories is as follows: "P's Delusion", "F's Accusation", "C's Will", "Y's Kidnapping", and the timeline is consistent with this.
[1069] Note: All copyrights of this translation belong to the original author YAMAMOTO Seiji. The Chinese translation and all annotations are added by the translator. Some annotation content refers to or quotes from related websites. No form of reproduction or commercial use is allowed.
[1070] 1
[1071] The "Lavinia" sightseeing ship, which departed from the port of Sunrise, is currently sailing smoothly along the waterway to Odaiba through Tokyo Bay, passing under the Rainbow Bridge.
[1072] The sunlight falls on the water, reflecting a patchwork of light and shadow. On the right side of the ship, numerous warehouses are lined up, and the red and white cranes stand tall like giant giraffes among them. On the left side of the ship, in the Odaiba district, there are modern hotels and TV towers. Further in the direction of Haneda Airport, airplanes are taking off and landing slowly.
[1073] In the bright sunlight, all of these exude a sense of tranquility in the autumn afternoon.

Her lustrous, straight hair shines in the sunlight, complementing her already pale complexion. Even Mizuho, a fellow woman, is mesmerized by this pose. Mizuho is dressed in a beige waistcoat and blue jeans.
[1077] Passengers nearby occasionally glance in the direction of Chikako and Mizuho.

[1091] Note 2: A suspension bridge in Tokyo Bay that connects the Minato ward's Asakusa and Odaiba. The official name is Tokyo Port Link Bridge. The bridge is 798 meters long, with a span of 570 meters. Construction began in 1987 and was completed in 1993. It opened on August 26, 1993.

It would then turn west and return to the Asakusa Pier. The total travel time is approximately four hours. At 4:00 PM and 6:00 PM, the ship's restaurant would serve afternoon tea and dinner respectively. Until then, passengers would be walking around the ship for entertainment.

[1536] "Just because the deceased is Japanese, does that mean she would always write the initial in the order of surname first, name second? I can't agree with that argument."
[1537] "In any case, the deceased died before writing what should have come after 'C'. So, the message she left is incomplete."
[1538] At this point, Rikako, who had been listening quietly, interjected in her usual light-hearted tone, "Excuse me, Tsukiyomi-san, but did the deceased really intend to write anything after 'C'? There's no letter after 'C', is there?"
[1539] "There's no letter after 'C'? Why do you think that, Rikako-san?" asked Tetsuya.
[1540] "If the deceased wanted to write both 'C' and another letter, it would take too much time and she might not finish before dying. I think Tsukiyomi-san understood that. [1541] "The part that does not start with C? But the deceased left C."
[1542] "Lady Thousand-Year Cherry did not intend to write C, but to leave another letter – the first letter of a surname or a name that does not start with C. However, she died during the process of writing, and it appears that she wrote C. What do you think?"
[1543] "Died during the process of writing another letter? For example?"

[1545] "Ah, I see now. [1546] However, there was a different opinion at this point.

The ship turned from the southeast course to the north and sailed around the island in a clockwise direction. At that time, the sightseeing ship circled around the Sea Fireflies Island by about 225 degrees. Along with this rotation, the table at the crime scene also moved by the corresponding degree. That is, the light spot on the tablecloth traced out a circular burn mark with the glass vase as the center, about 225 degrees in length. That is the C-shaped burn mark."
[1595] "Ah... " Mingshi imagined the scene at that time and was amazed by its grandeur."
[1596] "If it were a smaller ship, the rotation would have ended quickly, and the light dots on the tablecloth would have moved rapidly, leaving no time for the tablecloth to be burned. Moreover, as it is a sightseeing ship, it should rotate more slowly to allow tourists to get a closer look at the Sea Lanterns Artificial Island. Therefore, the light dots on the tablecloth would move very slowly, thus creating a C-shaped burn mark."
[1597] "Natural phenomenon... In the end, C has no meaning at all..."

Therefore, because Chikurabetsu boarded the ship on the day of the event, he was locked as the suspect from the beginning."

[2752] To carry out a kidnapping, the perpetrator must be familiar with the victim's family situation and assets, as well as the victim's daily routine.
[2753] Therefore, the perpetrator will likely target a wealthy family that is closer to them.
[2754] Although kidnappings due to resentment do occur, in those cases, the target is more likely to be a family closer to the perpetrator.
[2755] However, my family has no connection with Reiya.

The boy's name was Satsuki Yoshizawa, the only son of Satsuki Sasaki and Hanae Sasaki. Satsuki Sasaki passed away at the age of 46 in April 2004 due to pancreatic cancer, and he wrote this note before his death. This website introduces his notes, and we are the administrators, Fujimoto Toshihiro and Yuzuki couple, Fujimoto is a friend of Satsuki Sasaki, and Yuzuki is the younger sister of Hanae Sasaki. We are releasing his notes on this website in accordance with Satsuki Sasaki's wish. Twelve years ago, a tragedy struck a happy family in the spring, and we want more people to know about this event and hope to solve the case with everyone's help. Please provide any information or tips you may have."

In reality, Tadashi had murdered Tsubaki. Since Tsubaki had already known that Yusuke and Tadashi were not related by blood, Tadashi's true motive was to kill Yusuke.
